 Prosperous political paradox: The intangible secular ideal of this nation, which sought to depict an anthropomorphic image and etched its body on the map of the country, contained a rich political paradox in the process
 deviyon or devataaon se pati padi is dharti par is nai devi kaa aavirbhaav beesvin sadi ke aarambh main hota he jo khud apane liye ek jagah banaati he

 isane hamaare bhugolic or prashasnic daawey ko nae sire se shuchita pradaan karne kaa kaam kiya
 The difference between her body and the map gradually faded, then Bharat Mata started collecting other national secular symbols around her like the tricolor and the Ashoka pillar
 kabhi-kabhi to yah mishrit paridrishy itnaa doordarshee ban padaa he ki isse aakarshith hue bina rah paanaa mushkil ho jaataa he

 True patriotism will not emerge among our countrymen until they can envision a motherland ‚Äî we have to give it the form of a goddess! ‚Äùin this way a woman became a goddess and the motherland was depicted with a picture of a goddess, Which emerges from the map of India and accepts the sacrifice of her martyred sons

 Today we stand at the far end of the country's history, where we are forced to ask ourselves the question, why did this second hypothesis of the nation fail to live on the ground?  rashtriya khelon main yojit spardhaon kaa shanivaar teble tennis pratiyogitaaon ke final ke saath samaapan ho gaya jiske baad padak talika main sena 70 swarna, 50 rajat or 42 kaansya padakon ke saath kul 162 padak jitkar sheersh par rahi jabaki iske baad manipur ne kul 48 swarna, 37 rajat or 33 kaansya padakon ke saath 118 padak jite
 a total of three union territories did not receive any medals in these games concluded on Saturday and will have to return empty handed, including Pondicherry Diu and Daman and Dadar Nagar Haveli
 khelon main teen-teen rajyon ke alaava chah aise rajya bhi the jinhen ek bhi swarna padak hasil nahin ho sakaa
 Thus, out of the 35 teams involved in the overall game, nine teams did not lose a single gold medal
 rashtriya khelon main kul 444 swarna, 447 rajat or 588 kaansya samet 1479 padakon kaa faisla hua
 Apart from the Union Territories returning empty-handed, the states which could not get a single gold medal included Nagaland Mizoram Chandigarh Arunachal Gujarat and Jammu Kashmir

 ) The word 'harijan' will be removed from the names and addresses of government schools in Rajasthan
 rajya ke shiksha vibhaag ne isaki kavayad shuru kar di he or un skulon kii suchi maangi he jinke naam main 'harijan' shabd aata he
 The state's Director of Secondary Education has sent a letter to all the Chief District Education Officers and ex-officio District Project Coordinators of Samagra Shiksha Abhiyan
 isamen adhikariyon se kaha gaya he ki ve apane adhinsth sanchalit aise rajkeey vidyalayon ke naam sanshodhan ke prastaav gelevaar samekit kar bhejein taaki samekit prastaav sweekruti ke liye aage sarkaar ko bhijwaaye ja saken
 Director of Secondary Education Nathmal Didel told 'bhasha' that in writing a letter to all the Chief District Education Officers of the state and coordinators of the District Composite Education Campaign, such proposals have been sought that how many such schools are there in the name 'harijan' Has been used
 isamen naam parivartan ke liye sarkaar apni sweekruti pradaan karegi
 The government gives approval to amend a name
 ambedkar shiksha sadan samiti lunkarnsar sahit kuch sansthaaon ne sarkari skulon ke naam main harijan shabd ke istemaal par aapatti jataate hue ise hataane kii maang kii thi
 These institutions have termed the use of the word 'harijan' as unconstitutional
 didel ne bataaya ki sriganganagar main ek vidhyalay kaa naam rajkeey ucch madhyamik vidhyalay, harijan basti (sriganganagar) likhaa hua he
 After receiving a memorandum to change the name of this school, we have issued a circular for the Chief District Education Officers and ex-officio District Project Coordinators
 adhikariyon se kaha gaya he ki kisi bhi jile main aisa koi skool he to iske sambandh main jaankaree den

 unhone kaha ki rajya main mere dhyaan main aisa koi skool nahin he jinke naam main 'harijan' shabd kaa prayog kiya gaya he
 Generally, the name of state schools is associated with the name of a great person, freedom fighter or a martyr in the country, but people object to the use of the word 'harijan' in their address along with the name of the school
 ambedkar shiksha sadan samiti bikaner kii ore se 11 sitambar ko bheje gaye gyaapan ke anusaar rajya kshetra main aise kai rajkeey vidhyalay aise he jinke saath harijan basti / harijan mohalla kaa ullekh kiya gaya he
 The memorandum states that the word 'harijan' is not a constitutional word
 yah dalit samaaj ke maan sammaan ke virudv he tathaa is varg ke logon main hinabhaavna paidaa karata he
